## 1.1.0 (2024-06-14)


### Features

* [#1000](https://github.com/biocypher/biochatter-next/issues/1000) client-side only and desktop app ([a023308](https://github.com/biocypher/biochatter-next/commit/a023308d52a14e1d43d51558dec61dc1253064cc))
